# P0-K5 — Corrupt Key File Fails Fast [ACCEPTANCE]

Who: The security reviewer.

What: The security reviewer corrupts the signing key file to simulate disk
damage or tampering. When the broker restarts, it must refuse to start
and print a clear error message. It must NOT silently generate a new key.

Why: Silent key regeneration invalidates all tokens with no explanation.

How to run: Stop broker, corrupt key via volume mount, restart, check logs.

Expected: Broker exits non-zero, logs show signing key error, health fails.
